<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Net revenues decreased 0.6%; Organic Net Revenue<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> grew 0.6% </TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Returned approximately $800&nbsp;million in capital to shareholders </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#150;
May&nbsp;2, 2017 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) today reported its first quarter 2017 results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We had a
solid start to the year despite challenging market conditions,&#148; said Irene Rosenfeld, Chairman and CEO. &#147;We delivered both <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> organic growth and strong margin expansion in the quarter, while
also making critical investments for our future. We remain confident&nbsp;in&nbsp;and committed to our balanced&nbsp;strategy for both <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-</FONT> and bottom-line growth, continuing to focus on what we can control to
deliver long-term value creation for our shareholders.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Net Revenue </B></P>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Net revenues</B> decreased 0.6&nbsp;percent, driven by currency headwinds. Organic Net Revenue increased 0.6&nbsp;percent, with growth in all regions except North America. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Gross profit margin</B> was 39.4&nbsp;percent, an increase of 10 basis points driven primarily by lower Restructuring Program implementation costs. Adjusted Gross Profit margin was 40.3&nbsp;percent, a decrease of 20
basis points, driven by unfavorable mix impacts and higher input costs, partially offset by strong net productivity and improved pricing. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Operating income margin</B> was 13.1&nbsp;percent, up 190 basis points, reflecting the Adjusted Operating Income gains and the benefit from the settlement of a Cadbury tax matter. Adjusted Operating Income margin
increased 90 basis points to 16.8&nbsp;percent due primarily to continued reductions in overhead costs and supply chain productivity savings. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Diluted EPS</B> was $0.41, up 17&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by operating gains and the benefit from the settlement of a Cadbury tax matter. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Adjusted EPS</B> was $0.53 and grew 6&nbsp;percent on a constant-currency basis, driven primarily by operating gains. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Capital Return</B>: The company repurchased over $470&nbsp;million of its common stock and paid approximately $300&nbsp;million in cash dividends. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2017 Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International
provides guidance on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, as the company cannot predict some elements that are included in reported GAAP results, including the impact of foreign exchange. Refer to the Outlook section in the
discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures below for more details. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company continues to expect
Organic Net Revenue to increase at least 1&nbsp;percent in 2017 and Adjusted Operating Income margin in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-16&nbsp;percent</FONT> range. The company also expects double-digit Adjusted EPS growth on a
constant-currency basis. The company estimates currency translation would reduce net revenue growth by approximately 1 percent<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> and Adjusted EPS by approximately $0.02<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>. In addition, the company expects Free Cash Flow<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> of approximately $2&nbsp;billion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International will host a conference call for investors with accompanying slides to review its results at 5 p.m. ET today. A
listen-only webcast will be provided at <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U>. An archive of the webcast will be available on the company&#146;s web site. The company will be live tweeting the event at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) is building the best snacking company in the world, with 2016 net revenues of approximately
$26&nbsp;billion. Creating more moments of joy in approximately 165 countries, Mondel&#275;z International is a world leader in biscuits, chocolate, gum, candy and powdered beverages, featuring global Power Brands such as <I>Oreo </I>and<I> belVita
</I>biscuits<I>; Cadbury Dairy Milk</I> and <I>Milka</I> chocolate; and <I>Trident</I> gum.&nbsp;Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, NASDAQ 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit
<U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U> or follow the company on Twitter at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>End Notes </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

currency are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. Please see discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures at the end of this press release for more information. </TD></TR></TABLE>

</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Power Brands include some of the company&#146;s largest global and regional brands, such as <I>Oreo</I>, <I>Chips Ahoy!</I>, <I>Ritz,
TUC/Club Social</I> and <I>belVita</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk, Milka</I> and <I>Lacta</I> chocolate; <I>Trident</I> gum; <I>Halls</I> candy; and <I>Tang</I> powdered beverages. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Emerging markets consist of the Latin America region in its entirety; the Asia, Middle East and Africa region excluding Australia, New Zealand
and Japan; and the following countries from the Europe region: Russia, Ukraine, Turkey, Kazakhstan, Belarus, Georgia, Poland, Czech Republic, Slovak Republic, Hungary, Bulgaria, Romania, the Baltics and the East Adriatic countries. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Developed markets include the entire North America region, the Europe region excluding the countries included in the emerging markets
definition, and Australia, New Zealand and Japan from the Asia, Middle East and Africa region.</P>

&#147;expect,&#148; &#147;may,&#148; &#147;would,&#148; &#147;could,&#148; &#147;believe,&#148; &#147;estimate,&#148; &#147;deliver,&#148; &#147;guidance,&#148; &#147;outlook&#148; and similar expressions are intended to identify the company&#146;s
forward-looking statements, including, but not limited to, statements about: the company&#146;s future performance, including its future revenue growth, earnings per share, margins and cash flow; currency and the effect of foreign exchange
translation on the company&#146;s results of operations; the company&#146;s growth strategy; the sale of most of the company&#146;s grocery business in Australia and New Zealand; value creation for shareholders; the costs of, timing of expenditures
under and completion of the company&#146;s restructuring program; and the company&#146;s outlook, including 2017 Organic Net Revenue growth, Adjusted Operating Income margin, Adjusted EPS and Free Cash Flow. These forward-looking statements are
subject to a number of risks and uncertainties, many of which are beyond the company&#146;s control, which could cause the company&#146;s actual results to differ materially from those indicated in the company&#146;s forward-looking statements. Such
factors include, but are not limited to, risks from operating globally including in emerging markets; changes in currency exchange rates, controls and restrictions; continued volatility of commodity and other input costs; weakness in economic
conditions; weakness in consumer spending; pricing actions; unanticipated disruptions to the company&#146;s business; competition; the restructuring program and the company&#146;s other transformation initiatives not yielding the anticipated
benefits; changes in the assumptions on which the restructuring program is based; and tax law changes. Please also see the company&#146;s risk factors, as they may be amended from time to time, set forth in its filings with the SEC, including the
company&#146;s most recently filed Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K.</FONT> Mondel&#275;z International disclaims and does not undertake any obligation to update or revise any forward-looking statement in this press

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Reconciliation of GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>(Unaudited) </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company reports its
financial results in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#147;GAAP&#148;). However, management believes that also presenting certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
provides additional information to facilitate comparison of the company&#146;s historical operating results and trends in its underlying operating results, and provides additional transparency on how the company evaluates its business. Management
uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in making financial, operating and planning decisions and in evaluating the company&#146;s performance. The company also believes that presenting these measures allows
investors to view its performance using the same measures that the company uses in evaluating its financial and business performance and trends. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
company considers quantitative and qualitative factors in assessing whether to adjust for the impact of items that may be significant or that could affect an understanding of its ongoing financial and business performance and trends. The adjustments
generally fall within the following categories: acquisition&nbsp;&amp; divestiture activities, gains and losses on intangible asset sales and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairments, major program restructuring activities,
constant currency and related adjustments, major program financing and hedging activities and other major items affecting comparability of operating results. See below for a description of adjustments to the company&#146;s U.S. GAAP financial
measures included herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> information should be considered as supplemental in nature and is not meant to
be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP. In addition, the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may not be the same as or
comparable to similar <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures presented by other companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Because GAAP financial measures on a
forward-looking basis are not accessible and reconciling information is not available without unreasonable effort, the company has not provided that information with regard to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
in the company&#146;s outlook. Refer to the Outlook section below for more details. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>DEFINITIONS OF THE COMPANY&#146;S <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and corresponding metrics reflect how the company evaluates its
operating results currently and provide improved comparability of operating results. As new events or circumstances arise, these definitions could change over time. When these definitions change, the company provides the updated definitions and
presents the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> historical results on a comparable basis <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(1)</SUP>. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">&#147;Organic Net Revenue&#148; is defined as net revenues excluding the impacts of acquisitions, divestitures <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(2)</SUP>; the historical global coffee business <SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(3)</SUP>; the historical Venezuelan operations; accounting calendar changes; and currency rate fluctuations <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(4)</SUP>. The company believes that Organic Net
Revenue reflects the underlying growth from the ongoing activities of its business and provides improved comparability of results. The company also evaluates Organic Net Revenue growth from emerging markets and its Power Brands. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(5)</SUP>; acquisition integration costs; incremental costs associated with the Jacobs Douwe Egberts (&#147;JDE&#148;) coffee business transactions; the operating results of divestitures <SUP

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivative contracts <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(6)</SUP>. The company also presents &#147;Adjusted Gross Profit
margin,&#148; which is subject to the same adjustments as Adjusted Gross Profit. The company believes that Adjusted Gross Profit and Adjusted Gross Profit margin provide improved comparability of underlying operating results. The company also
evaluates growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted Gross Profit on a constant currency basis <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(4)</SUP>. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivative contracts <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(6)</SUP>; equity method
investment earnings historically reported within operating income <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(7)</SUP>; and the benefit from the settlement of a Cadbury tax matter <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(8)</SUP>. The
company also presents &#147;Adjusted Operating Income margin&#148; and &#147;Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin&#148;, which are subject to the same adjustments as Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment Operating Income. The company
believes that Adjusted Operating Income, Adjusted Segment Operating Income, Adjusted Operating Income margin and Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin provide improved comparability of underlying operating results. The company also evaluates
growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment Operating Income on a constant currency basis <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(4)</SUP>. </TD></TR></TABLE>

The company believes that Adjusted EPS provides improved comparability of underlying operating results. The company also evaluates growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted EPS on a constant currency basis

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">During the third quarter of 2016, the company began to exclude unrealized gains and losses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts) from outstanding
commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures until such time that the related exposures impact its operating results. Since the company purchases commodity and
forecasted currency contracts to mitigate price volatility primarily for inventory requirements in future periods, the company made this adjustment to remove the volatility of these future inventory purchases on current operating results to
facilitate comparisons of its underlying operating performance across periods. The company also discontinued designating commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives for hedge accounting treatment. To facilitate comparisons of the
company&#146;s underlying operating results, the company has recast all historical <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures to exclude the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts. </TD></TR></TABLE>

company does not have direct control over the operations or resulting revenue and expenses. The company&#146;s use of equity method investment net earnings on an adjusted basis is not intended to imply that the company has any such control. The

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SEGMENT OPERATING INCOME </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company uses segment operating income to evaluate segment performance and allocate resources. The company believes it is appropriate to disclose this
measure to help investors analyze segment performance and trends. Segment operating income excludes unrealized gains and losses on hedging activities (which are a component of cost of sales), general corporate expenses (which are a component of
selling, general and administrative expenses) and amortization of intangibles in all periods presented. The company excludes these items from segment operating income in order to provide better transparency of its segment operating results.
Furthermore, the company centrally manages interest and other expense, net. Accordingly, the company does not present these items by segment because they are excluded from the segment profitability measure that management reviews. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>ITEMS IMPACTING COMPARABILITY OF OPERATING RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information is provided to give qualitative and quantitative information related to items impacting comparability of operating results. The company determines which items to consider as &#147;items impacting comparability&#148; based on
how management views the company&#146;s business; makes financial, operating and planning decisions; and evaluates the company&#146;s ongoing performance. In addition, the company discloses the impact of changes in currency exchange rates on the
company&#146;s financial results in order to reflect results on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Divestitures </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On December&nbsp;1, 2016, the company completed the sale of a confectionery business in Costa Rica represented by a local brand. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Divestiture-related costs </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&nbsp;18,
2017, the company reached an agreement to sell most of its grocery business in Australia and New Zealand to Bega Cheese Limited. The transaction is expected to close in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-2017.</FONT> The company incurred
incremental expenses to ready the business for the sale transactions of $1&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April 28, 2017,
the company completed the sale of several manufacturing facilities in France and the sale or license of several local confectionery brands. The sale was subject to E.U. and local regulatory approvals, completion of employee consultation requirements
and additional steps to prepare the assets for transfer. In March 2017, the company recorded &#128;17&nbsp;million ($18&nbsp;million as of March&nbsp;31, 2017) of incremental expenses and an impairment of fixed assets primarily due to an agreed
reduction in the sales price. The company recorded these costs within cost of sales and selling, general and administrative expenses of its Europe segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Acquisitions and acquisition-related costs </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On
November&nbsp;2, 2016, the company purchased from Burton&#146;s Biscuit Company certain intangibles, which include the license to manufacture, market and sell Cadbury-branded biscuits in additional key markets around the world, including in the
United Kingdom, France, Ireland, North America and Saudi Arabia. The purchase added incremental net revenues of $14&nbsp;million (constant currency basis) in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Acquisition integration costs </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within the
company&#146;s AMEA segment, in connection with the acquisition of a biscuit operation in Vietnam, the company recorded integration costs of $1&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2017 and $3&nbsp;million in the three months ended
March&nbsp;31, 2016. The company recorded these acquisition integration costs in selling, general and administrative expenses. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>2014-2018 Restructuring Program </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On May&nbsp;6, 2014, the company&#146;s Board of Directors approved a $3.5&nbsp;billion restructuring program, comprised of approximately $2.5&nbsp;billion in
cash costs and $1&nbsp;billion in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> costs (&#147;2014-2018 Restructuring Program&#148;), and up to $2.2&nbsp;billion of capital expenditures. On August&nbsp;31, 2016, the company&#146;s Board of
Directors approved a reallocation within the program of $600&nbsp;million of previously approved capital expenditures to be spent on restructuring program cash costs. There was no change to the total $5.7&nbsp;billion of total program costs and no
change to the total $4.7&nbsp;billion of cash outlays. The $5.7&nbsp;billion total cost of the program is now comprised of approximately $4.1&nbsp;billion of restructuring program costs ($3.1&nbsp;billion cash costs and $1&nbsp;billion <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> costs) and up to $1.6&nbsp;billion of capital expenditures. The primary objective of the 2014-2018 Restructuring Program is to reduce the company&#146;s operating cost structure in both supply chain and
overhead costs. The program is intended primarily to cover severance as well as asset disposals and other manufacturing-related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> costs. Since inception, the company has incurred total restructuring and
related implementation charges of $2.7&nbsp;billion related to the 2014-2018 Restructuring Program. The company has incurred the majority of the program&#146;s charges through the first quarter of 2017 and expects to complete the program by <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Restructuring costs </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded restructuring charges of $157&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2017 and $139&nbsp;million in the three months ended
March&nbsp;31, 2016 within asset impairment and exit costs. These charges were for non-cash asset write-downs (including accelerated depreciation and asset impairments), severance and other related costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Implementation costs </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Implementation costs are directly
attributable to restructuring activities; however, they do not qualify for special accounting treatment as exit or disposal activities. Implementation costs primarily relate to reorganizing the company&#146;s operations and facilities in connection
with its supply chain reinvention program and other identified productivity and cost saving initiatives. The costs include incremental expenses related to the closure of facilities, costs to terminate certain contracts and the simplification of the
company&#146;s information systems. The company recorded implementation costs of $54&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2017 and $98&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2016. The company recorded these costs
within cost of sales and general corporate expense within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Gain on equity method investment exchange
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&nbsp;3, 2016, a subsidiary of Acorn Holdings B.V. (&#147;AHBV&#148;) completed the $13.9&nbsp;billion acquisition of all of the
outstanding common stock of Keurig Green Mountain, Inc. (&#147;Keurig&#148;) through a merger transaction. On March&nbsp;7, 2016, the company exchanged with a subsidiary of AHBV a portion of the company&#146;s equity interest in JDE with a carrying
value of &#128;1.7&nbsp;billion (approximately $2.0&nbsp;billion as of March&nbsp;7, 2016) for an interest in Keurig with a fair value of $2.0&nbsp;billion based on the merger consideration per share for Keurig. The company recorded the difference
between the fair value of Keurig and its basis in JDE shares as a $43&nbsp;million gain on the equity method investment exchange in March 2016. Immediately following the exchange, the company&#146;s ownership interest in JDE was 26.5% and its
interest in Keurig was 24.2%. The company accounts for its investments in JDE and Keurig under the equity method and recognizes its share of their earnings within equity method investment earnings and its share of their dividends within the
company&#146;s cash flows. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Equity method investee adjustments </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within Adjusted EPS, the company&#146;s equity method investment net earnings exclude its proportionate share of its investees&#146; unusual or infrequent
items, such as acquisition and divestiture-related costs and restructuring program costs. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from
commodity and currency derivative contracts </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the third quarter of 2016, the company began to exclude unrealized gains and losses <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts) from outstanding commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures
until such time that the related exposures impact its operating results. To facilitate comparisons of its underlying operating results, the company has recast all historical <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures to
exclude the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded net unrealized
losses on commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives of $51&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2017 and $54&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Loss related to interest rate swaps </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company
recognized <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> losses of $97&nbsp;million in the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2016, within interest and other expense, net related to certain U.S. dollar interest rate swaps that the company no longer
designated as accounting cash flow hedges due to a change in financing plans. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Intangible assets gains and losses </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&nbsp;31, 2016, the company recorded a $14&nbsp;million impairment charge for a gum&nbsp;&amp; candy trademark as a portion of its carrying value would
not be recoverable based on future cash flows expected under a planned license agreement with the buyer. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Benefit from the settlement of Cadbury tax
matter </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As part of the company&#146;s 2010 Cadbury acquisition, the company became the responsible party for tax matters under a February&nbsp;2,
2006 dated Deed of Tax Covenant (&#147;Tax Indemnity&#148;) between the Cadbury Schweppes PLC and related entities (&#147;Schweppes&#148;) and Black Lion Beverages and related entities. The tax matters included an ongoing transfer pricing case with
the Spanish tax authorities related to the Schweppes businesses Cadbury divested prior to the company&#146;s acquisition of Cadbury. During the first quarter of 2017, the Spanish Supreme Court decided the case in the company&#146;s favor. As a
result of the final ruling, during the first quarter of 2017, the company recorded a favorable earnings impact of $46&nbsp;million in selling, general and administrative expenses and $12&nbsp;million in interest and other expense, net, for a total <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> impact of $58&nbsp;million due to the reversal of Cadbury-related accrued liabilities related to this matter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Constant currency </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management evaluates the
operating performance of the company and its international subsidiaries on a constant currency basis. The company determines its constant currency operating results by dividing or multiplying, as appropriate, the current period local currency
operating results by the currency exchange rates used to translate the company&#146;s financial statements in the comparable prior-year period to determine what the current period U.S. dollar operating results would have been if the currency
exchange rate had not changed from the comparable prior-year period. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>OUTLOOK </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
company&#146;s outlook for 2017 Organic Net Revenue growth, Adjusted Operating Income margin, Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis and Free Cash Flow are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude or
otherwise adjust for items impacting comparability of financial results such as the impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates, restructuring activities, acquisitions and divestitures. The company is not able to reconcile its full year
2017 projected Organic Net Revenue growth to its full year 2017 projected reported net revenue growth because the company is unable to predict the 2017 impact of foreign exchange due to the unpredictability of future changes in foreign exchange
rates, which could be material as a significant portion of the company&#146;s operations are outside the U.S. The company is not able to reconcile its full year 2017 projected Adjusted Operating Income margin to its full year 2017 projected reported
operating income margin because the company is unable to predict the timing of its Restructuring Program costs, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted
currency transaction derivative contracts and impacts from potential acquisitions or divestitures. The company is not able to reconcile its full year 2017 projected Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis to its full year 2017 projected
reported diluted EPS growth because the company is unable to predict the timing of its Restructuring Program costs, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency forecasted derivative
contracts, impacts from potential acquisitions or divestitures as well as the impact of foreign exchange due to the unpredictability of future changes in foreign exchange rates, which could be material as a significant portion of the company&#146;s
operations are outside the U.S. The company is not able to reconcile its full year 2017 projected Free Cash Flow to its full year 2017 projected net cash from operating activities because the company is unable to predict the timing and amount of
capital expenditures impacting cash flow. Therefore, because of the uncertainty and variability of the nature and amount of future adjustments, which could be significant, the company is unable to provide a reconciliation of these measures without
unreasonable effort. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>

<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><U>Schedule 4b </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><U>Schedule 8 </U></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Reconciliation of GAAP to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Segment Data </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions of U.S.
dollars) (Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
